
! Proper nouns

! Continuation lexica
! Personal names

! Continuation lexica
! ===================

! Continuation lexica for personal names
! --------------------------------------


! At the moment, these continuation lexica are identical. But since I
! suspect that linguistic input will prove that the words behave
! differently, they are kept distinct.

! Names from Sweden

LEXICON NAME ! these are the non-vow-final names from Sweden
CNAME_EVEN ;

! Vowel final names
! - - - - - - - - -

LEXICON VNAME_ODD ! Names ending in stressless vowel
+N+Prop+Sg: N_ODD_SG ;
+N+Prop+Pl: N_ODD_PL ;
+N+Prop:    N_ODD_ESS ;
+N+Prop+Attr: FINAL1 ;

LEXICON VNAME_EVEN ! Names ending in stressless vowel
+N+Prop+Sg: NIEJTE_SG ;
+N+Prop+Pl: NIEJTE_PL ;
+N+Prop:    EVEN_ESS ;
+N+Prop+Attr: FINAL1 ;


! Consonant final names
! - - - - - - - - -

! LEXICON CNAME_ODD ! Names ending in stressless vowel (still) not in use
!  +N+Prop+Sg: CNAME_ODD_SG ; ! name special
!  +N+Prop+Pl: N_ODD_PL ;     ! normal noun
!  +N+Prop:    N_ODD_ESS ;    ! normal noun
!  +N+Prop+Attr: FINAL1 ;     ! name special

LEXICON CNAME_EVEN ! Names ending in stressless vowel
+N+Prop+Sg: NIEJTE_SG ;
+N+Prop+Pl: NIEJTE_PL ;
+N+Prop:    EVEN_ESS ;
+N+Prop+Attr: FINAL1 ;


LEXICON NYSTØ ! Names ending in stressed vowel, typically scand. compounds 
VNAME ; ! check whether this is correct!


LEXICON SNAME_ODD ! Southern Sami names
VNAME_ODD ;

! Even syllable Sámi names:
LEXICON PN_IE ! as N_IE, but with Prop tag
+N+Prop+Sg: N_IE_SG ;
+N+Prop+Pl: N_IE_PL ;
+N+Prop:    N_IE_ESS ;
+N+Prop+Attr: FINAL1 ;

! LEXICON PN_OE_UML ! as N_OE_UML, but with Prop tag ! (still) not in use
!  +N+Prop: N_OE_SGILL_UML ;
!           PN_OE ;

LEXICON PN_OE ! as N_OE, but with Prop tag
+N+Prop+Sg: N_OE_SG ;
+N+Prop+Pl: N_OE_PL ;
+N+Prop:    N_OE_ESS ;
+N+Prop+Attr: FINAL1 ;

LEXICON SNAME_MAANA ! as MAANA, but with Prop tag
+N+Prop+Sg: MAANA_SG ;
+N+Prop+Pl: MAANA_PL ;
+N+Prop:    EVEN_ESS ;
+N+Prop+Attr: FINAL1 ;

LEXICON SNAME_NIEJTE ! as NIEJTE, but with Prop tag
+N+Prop+Sg: NIEJTE_SG ;
+N+Prop+Pl: NIEJTE_PL ;
+N+Prop:    EVEN_ESS ;
+N+Prop+Attr: FINAL1 ;


! Old names, for backwards compatibility until all entries have got new names
! ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

LEXICON CNAME
CNAME_EVEN ; ! Even syllable as default - rename using either CNAME_EVEN or
! CNAME_ODD.

LEXICON VNAME
SNAME_NIEJTE ; ! Even syllable as default - rename using either VNAME_ODD, or
! the appropriate even syllable lexicons.

! ==========
